    const rightTitleElementPC = containerElement.querySelector(".image-swap-slide-bar__right-title-box > .image-swap-slide-bar__right-text-box-title");

    const leftContentElementsPC = containerElement.querySelectorAll(".image-swap-slide-bar__left-title-pc > .image-swap-slide-bar__recommend-li");
    const rightContentElementsPC = containerElement.querySelectorAll(".image-swap-slide-bar__right-title-pc > .image-swap-slide-bar__recommend-li");


    // for mobile
    
    const leftTitleElementMobile = containerElement.querySelector(".image-swap-slide-bar__image-mobile-only-box > .ty-image-swap-slide-bar__mobile-title-left");
    const rightTitleElementMobile = containerElement.querySelector(".image-swap-slide-bar__image-mobile-only-box > .ty-image-swap-slide-bar__mobile-title-right");

    const leftContentElementsMobile = containerElement.querySelectorAll(".image-swap-slide-bar__left-title-mobile > .image-swap-slide-bar__recommend-li");
    const rightContentElementsMobile = containerElement.querySelectorAll(".image-swap-slide-bar__right-title-mobile > .image-swap-slide-bar__recommend-li");

    const touchCanvasElement = containerElement.querySelector(".image-swap-slide-bar-component");

    // only for relative mode
    var valueOnDragStart = 0;
    var slideOnDragStart = 0;
    
    const hideHintBar = () => {
      containerElement.querySelector(".image-swap-slide-bar-slideable-hint").classList.add("image-swap-slide-bar-slideable-hint-hidden");
    }

    const showHideElement = (element, isShow) => {
      if (!element) return;
      if (!isShow) element.classList.add("hidden") 
      else element.classList.remove("hidden")
    }

    const getElementXCenter = (element) => {
      if (!element) return;

      return (element.getBoundingClientRect().left + element.getBoundingClientRect().right) / 2
    }

    const identicalRealNickName = (index) => {
      if (index < 0) return;

      if (chipNickNamesList[index] === "") return true;
      if (chipNickNamesList[index].trim() === chipRealNamesList[index].trim()) return true;

      return false;
    }

    const calculateElementCenterDistance = (element, targetElement) => {
      if (!element) return;
      if (!targetElement) return;

      const elementCenter = getElementXCenter(element);
      const targetElementCenter = getElementXCenter(targetElement);

      return targetElementCenter - elementCenter
    }

    const calculateDistanceToShift = (calcElementIndex, centerElementIndex) => {
      if (calcElementIndex === centerElementIndex) return 0;
      const chipMargin = 15;
      const identicalNickName = identicalRealNickName(centerElementIndex);

      let distance = 0;

      chipNickNamesWidthList.forEach((chipWidth, chipIndex) => {
        if (calcElementIndex < centerElementIndex) {
          if (chipIndex < calcElementIndex) return ;
          if (chipIndex > centerElementIndex) return ;
          else if (chipIndex === calcElementIndex) { distance -= (chipWidth / 2); return ; }
          else if (chipIndex === centerElementIndex) { 
            if (identicalNickName) distance -= (chipWidth / 2);
            else distance -= (chipRealNamesWidthList[chipIndex] / 2); 
            distance -= chipMargin;
            return;
          }
          else { distance -= chipWidth + chipMargin; return; }
        } 
        
        else if (calcElementIndex > centerElementIndex) {
          if (chipIndex > calcElementIndex) return ;
          if (chipIndex < centerElementIndex) return ;
          else if (chipIndex === calcElementIndex) { distance += (chipWidth / 2); return; }
          else if (chipIndex === centerElementIndex) { 
            if (identicalNickName) distance += (chipWidth / 2); 
            else distance += (chipRealNamesWidthList[chipIndex] / 2); 
            distance += chipMargin;
            return;
          }
          else { distance += chipWidth + chipMargin; return; }
        }
      })

      return distance;
    }

    const lerp = (start, end, percent) => start * (1 - percent) + end * percent;

    const switchImage = (selectedIndex, hideBar, isManualSwitch) => {
      
        if (hideBar) hideHintBar();
      

      
        if (isManualSwitch) clearInterval(autoSwitchIntervalId);
      

      // prevent from moving out of range
      if (selectedIndex < 0) { selectedIndex = 0 }
      else if (selectedIndex > totalSlides - 1) { selectedIndex = totalSlides - 1 }

      if (currentSelectedChip === selectedIndex) return;
      currentSelectedChip = selectedIndex;
      
      // SWAP IMAGE
      imgElementList.forEach((element, index) => showHideElement(element, index === +selectedIndex));

      const identicalChipName = identicalRealNickName(selectedIndex);

      // SHIFT CHIPS
      chipsList.forEach((element, index) => {
        element.classList.remove("hidden-opacity-zero");
        
        if (index === +selectedIndex) {
          if (identicalChipName) element.classList.add("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dial-chips__selected")
          else element.classList.add("hidden-opacity-zero")
        }
        else element.classList.remove("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dial-chips__selected")

        element.setAttribute("style", `transform: translateX(${calculateDistanceToShift(index, selectedIndex)}px);`)
      });

      chipsNickNamesList.forEach((element, index) => {
        if (index === +selectedIndex && !identicalChipName) element.classList.add("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dial-chips__selected")
        else element.classList.remove("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dial-chips__selected")

        element.setAttribute("style", `transform: translateX(${calculateDistanceToShift(index, selectedIndex)}px);`)
      });

      // SWITCH CPU GPU RECOMMENDATION
      leftContentElementsPC.forEach((element, index) => showHideElement(element, index === +selectedIndex))
      leftContentElementsMobile.forEach((element, index) => showHideElement(element, index === +selectedIndex))
      rightContentElementsPC.forEach((element, index) => showHideElement(element, index === +selectedIndex))
      rightContentElementsMobile.forEach((element, index) => showHideElement(element, index === +selectedIndex))

      // SWITCH TITLES
      leftTitleElementPC.innerHTML = leftTitlesList[selectedIndex] || "";
      rightTitleElementPC.innerHTML = rightTitlesList[selectedIndex] || "";

      leftTitleElementMobile.innerHTML = leftTitlesList[selectedIndex] || "";
      rightTitleElementMobile.innerHTML = rightTitlesList[selectedIndex] || "";
    }

    const switchNextImage = (isManualSwitch) => {
      if (currentSelectedChip === totalSlides - 1) currentSelectedChip = -1;
      switchImage(currentSelectedChip + 1, isManualSwitch, isManualSwitch);
    }

    chipsList.forEach((element, index) => {
      element.addEventListener("click", () => switchImage(index, true, true));
      chipNickNamesWidthList.push(element.getBoundingClientRect().width);
    })

    chipsNickNamesList.forEach((element, index) => {
      chipRealNamesWidthList.push(element.getBoundingClientRect().width);
    })

    if (touchCanvasElement) {
        // Mobile Version
        touchCanvasElement.addEventListener("touchmove", (e) => {
          // console.log(e.target)
          
          if (!e.target) return;
          if (e.target.classList.contains("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dials")) return;
          if (e.target.classList.contains("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dial-chips")) return;
          if (e.target.classList.contains("image-swap-slide-bar__dial-extension")) return;
          
          const elementBoundingBox = touchCanvasElement.getBoundingClientRect();
          const elementX = elementBoundingBox.x;
          const elementWidth = elementBoundingBox.width;
          const touchX = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;

          
            //const lerpedPercentage = lerp( -0.3, 1.3, (1 - realPercentage));
            const realPercentage = (touchX - elementX) / elementWidth;
            const lerpedPercentage = lerp( -0.3, 1.3, realPercentage);
            switchImage(Math.floor(lerpedPercentage * totalSlides), true, true);
          
        })

        let mousePressed = false;

        touchCanvasElement.addEventListener("touchstart", (e) => {
          const touchX = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;
          
          // only for relative mode
          valueOnDragStart = touchX;
          slideOnDragStart = currentSelectedChip;
        });

        touchCanvasElement.addEventListener("mouseup", (e) => {
            if(e.which === 1) mousePressed = false;
        });

        document.addEventListener("mouseup", (e) => {
            if(e.which === 1) mousePressed = false;
        });
      
        touchCanvasElement.addEventListener("mousedown", (e) => {
            if(e.which === 1) mousePressed = true;
          
            const imageElement = containerElement.querySelector(".image-swap-slide-bar__image:not(.hidden)");

            if (imageElement) {
              const elementBoundingBox = imageElement.getBoundingClientRect();
              const elementX = elementBoundingBox.x;
              const elementWidth = elementBoundingBox.width;
              const mouseX = event.clientX - elementX;

              // Check if mouse is hovering on image
              if (mouseX >= elementWidth ) return;
              if (mouseX <= 0 ) return;

              // PREVENT SELECTING TEXT IF CLICKING ON IMAGE
              e.preventDefault();

              // only for relative mode
              valueOnDragStart = mouseX;
              slideOnDragStart = currentSelectedChip;
            }
        });
      
        // Desktop Version
        touchCanvasElement.addEventListener("mousemove", (e) => {
          // console.log(e.target)

          if (!mousePressed) return;
          
          if (!e.target) return;
          if (e.target.classList.contains("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dials")) return;
          if (e.target.classList.contains("image-swap-slide-bar__top-dial-chips")) return;
          if (e.target.classList.contains("image-swap-slide-bar__dial-extension")) return;

          const imageElement = containerElement.querySelector(".image-swap-slide-bar__image:not(.hidden)");
        
          if (imageElement) {
            const elementBoundingBox = imageElement.getBoundingClientRect();
            const elementX = elementBoundingBox.x;
            const elementY = elementBoundingBox.y;
            const elementWidth = elementBoundingBox.width;
            const elementHeight = elementBoundingBox.height;
            const mouseX = event.clientX - elementX;

            // Check if mouse is hovering on image
            if (mouseX >= elementWidth ) return;
            if (mouseX <= 0 ) return;

            
              // const realTouchPercentage = 1 - mouseX / elementWidth;
              const realTouchPercentage = mouseX / elementWidth;
      
              switchImage(Math.round(realTouchPercentage * totalSlides), true, true);
            
          }
        })
    } else {
      console.log("Failed to find touch canvas element")
    }

    switchImage(0, false, false);

    // for scroll mode
    
      autoSwitchIntervalId = setInterval(() => {
        switchNextImage(false)
      }, 2 * 1000)
    
  
    })()
</script>

                      Backward Compatibility on All Accessories
                    </h3><svg class="icon icon-caret" viewBox="0 0 10 6"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M9.354.646a.5.5 0 0 0-.708 0L5 4.293 1.354.646a.5.5 0 0 0-.708.708l4 4a.5.5 0 0 0 .708 0l4-4a.5.5 0 0 0 0-.708" clip-rule="evenodd"/></svg>
</summary>
                  <div
                    class="accordion__content rte"

                    aria-labelledby="Summary-collapsible_row_JVeQEm-template--24561355456830__8a93af34-f288-4295-ad78-15d728167cf4"

                  </div>

                    </h3><svg class="icon icon-caret" viewBox="0 0 10 6"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M9.354.646a.5.5 0 0 0-.708 0L5 4.293 1.354.646a.5.5 0 0 0-.708.708l4 4a.5.5 0 0 0 .708 0l4-4a.5.5 0 0 0 0-.708" clip-rule="evenodd"/></svg>
</summary>
                  <div
                    class="accordion__content rte"
                    id="CollapsibleAccordion-template--21191770997054__8a93af34-f288-4295-ad78-15d728167cf4-collapsible_row-3-template--24561355456830__8a93af34-f288-4295-ad78-15d728167cf4"
                    role="region"
                    aria-labelledby="Summary-template--21191770997054__8a93af34-f288-4295-ad78-15d728167cf4-collapsible_row-3-template--24561355456830__8a93af34-f288-4295-ad78-15d728167cf4"
